.opencode/specs/system-skill-advisor/003-skill-advisor-routing-engine/001-memory-search-routing-tuning/review/012-search-routing-final-review/review-report.md:18:1. Command-shaped `key_files` still survive parser sanitization and are then amplified into `entities.path`. `keepKeyFile()` rejects `node ...` and similar prefixes, but it does not reject `cd ... && npx vitest ...` strings, so those command lines still land in persisted metadata and `deriveEntities()` re-emits them as file-backed entities. The corpus scan found `59` command-shaped `derived.key_files` and `42` command-shaped `entities.path` values, including the reviewed 003 packet outputs. .opencode/specs/system-skill-advisor/003-skill-advisor-routing-engine/001-memory-search-routing-tuning/review/012-search-routing-final-review/review-report.md:24:2. The dedicated backfill verification lane still encodes the pre-refactor active-only default, so it fails against the shipped inclusive-default script. The script header and traversal logic say archived and future folders are included unless `--active-only` is passed, but `graph-metadata-backfill.vitest.ts` still expects the default scan to skip archived folders and phase `004-normalize-legacy-files` still documents that stale behavior. Running the test today fails 2 of 3 cases on that mismatch.
